executed that it deoptimized. When this happens, the base unspecialized
instruction is not counted.

Tier 1 instructions executed.

<td align="right">54.7%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">

</details>
</td>
<td align="right">11,411,174,639</td>
<td align="right">9.6%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
